```sql
use wheelhub
```

Commands completed successfully.



Total execution time: 00:00:00.013


<img src="https://i.postimg.cc/Y9wqyX3q/Commands-Category.png" alt="Sample Image" width="300" height="200">

**In SQL queries, clauses are executed based on the following order:**

- FROM and/or JOIN clause.
- WHERE clause.
- GROUP BY clause.
- HAVING clause.
- SELECT clause.
- DISTINCT clause.
- ORDER BY clause.
- LIMIT and/or OFFSET clause.

[https://www.shiksha.com/online-courses/articles/order-of-execution-in-sql/](https:\www.shiksha.com\online-courses\articles\order-of-execution-in-sql\)



```sql
SELECT
    *
FROM
    sales.customers;
```

ae</td><td>Carney</td></tr><tr><td>Sebrina</td><td>Hart</td></tr><tr><td>Kristofer</td><td>Craig</td></tr><tr><td>Luciana</td><td>Mcgee</td></tr><tr><td>Nicki</td><td>Fry</td></tr><tr><td>Devin</td><td>Shaffer</td></tr><tr><td>Erlinda</td><td>Osborne</td></tr><tr><td>Camila</td><td>Carroll</td></tr><tr><td>Vicki</td><td>Wiggins</td></tr><tr><td>Lois</td><td>Steele</td></tr><tr><td>Carola</td><td>Mcpherson</td></tr><tr><td>Rochell</td><td>Cantrell</td></tr><tr><td>Kasha</td><td>Sullivan</td></tr><tr><td>Viva</td><td>Dawson</td></tr><tr><td>Hue</td><td>Dalton</td></tr><tr><td>Andria</td><td>Rivers</td></tr><tr><td>Hilary</td><td>Savage</td></tr><tr><td>Lavona</td><td>Austin</td></tr><tr><td>Doreatha</td><td>Ford</td></tr><tr><td>Alina</td><td>Mcleod</td></tr><tr><td>Aide</td><td>Franco</td></tr><tr><td>Genny</td><td>Hensley</td></tr><tr><td>Melita</td><td>Dominguez</td></tr><tr><td>Fannie</td><td>Jenkins</td></tr><tr><td>Bobbi</td><td>Banks</td></tr><tr><td>Gwenn</td><td>Melton</td></tr><tr><td>Laci</td><td>Castro</td></tr><tr><td>Evelina</td><td>Manning</td></tr><tr><td>Tania</td><td>Swanson</td></tr><tr><td>Laurel</td><td>Schultz</td></tr><tr><td>Carolyne</td><td>Conley</td></tr><tr><td>Eldridge</td><td>Greer</td></tr><tr><td>Margret</td><td>Barnett</td></tr><tr><td>Oliva</td><td>Blackwell</td></tr><tr><td>Oralia</td><td>Farley</td></tr><tr><td>Romaine</td><td>Salazar</td></tr><tr><td>Hermila</td><td>Mckay</td></tr><tr><td>Lloyd</td><td>Miranda</td></tr><tr><td>Mandi</td><td>Gibbs</td></tr><tr><td>Hue</td><td>May</td></tr><tr><td>Tomika</td><td>Wilder</td></tr><tr><td>Graig</td><td>Roth</td></tr><tr><td>Lamar</td><td>Greer</td></tr><tr><td>Raymonde</td><td>Garcia</td></tr><tr><td>Cira</td><td>Downs</td></tr><tr><td>Marisa</td><td>Chambers</td></tr><tr><td>Rod</td><td>Hatfield</td></tr><tr><td>Quyen</td><td>Houston</td></tr><tr><td>Han</td><td>Schneider</td></tr><tr><td>Terrell</td><td>Mathis</td></tr><tr><td>Spring</td><td>Hayes</td></tr><tr><td>Lecia</td><td>Hancoc SELECT
```sql
    city,
    COUNT (*)
FROM
    sales.customers
WHERE
    state = 'CA'
GROUP BY
    city
ORDER BY
    city;
```

```sql
SELECT
    city,
    COUNT (*) counts_of_customers
FROM
    sales.customers
WHERE
    state = 'CA'
GROUP BY
    city
HAVING
    COUNT (*) > 10
ORDER BY
    city;
```


(5 rows affected)



Total execution time: 00:00:00.020

**Offset  and  FETCH  clauases:**  

- <span style="color: var(--vscode-foreground);">OFFSET&nbsp; &nbsp;clause&nbsp; number of rows to skip</span>
- FETCH  clause shoule be specify  the  number of rows  we can use  after OFFSET
- OFFSET   clause is mandatory first then FETCH  is an optional  later

**SELECT  TOP**  clause to get top  rows either by number or persent

  

```
SELECT TOP <no> col_names from <table_name> ORDER  BY <column_name>
```


```sql
SELECT 
    *
FROM
    production.products
ORDER BY
    list_price DESC
```
